    var omni = {

    "fbref" : s_omni.getQueryParam('fb_ref'),
    "sourceid" : s_omni.getQueryParam('sourceid'),

    getCampaignId : function() {

        else if (this.fbref) { return this.fbref.split('_')[1]; }
        else if (this.sourceid){ return this.sourceid; }
        else { return ''; }
        }
    };
